### Field and Region Recovery Variables

Oil recovery factors (or efficiency) may be reported at both the field and the region levels using a variety of parameters as summarized in and equations to . In addition to the actual recovery factors the simulator can also report the oil volumes produced by various drive mechanisms as described in the table.

See also section [[11.2.4](#anchor-5)[Field, Group, Well, Well Connection, and Completion Variables](#anchor-5)](#11.2.5.Field, Group, Well, Well Connection, and Completion Summary Variables|outline) that outlines the field production data summary variables, and section [[11.2.6](#anchor-6)[Field, Region, and Block Variables](#anchor-6)](#11.2.5.Field, Region, and Block Summary Variables|outline) that outlines the field, region and block production and injection data summary variables.

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Field and Region Summary Recovery Variables                                                                                    |                                                                 |        |         |          |                                                                                   |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                                                 |        |         |          |                                                                                   |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Type                                                                                                                           | > Variable                                                      | > Root | > Field | > Region | > Comment                                                                         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Recovery Efficiency (STOIIP)                              | > OE   | > FOE   | > ROE    | > Based on STOIIP.                                                                |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Recovery Efficiency (Wells)                               | > OEW  | > FOEW  | > ROEW   | > Based on well production and STOIIP.                                            |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Recovery Efficiency (STOIIP Mobile with Respect to Water) | > OEIW | > FOEIW | > ROEIW  | > Based on STOIIP and initial mobile oil saturate with respect to water.          |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Recovery Efficiency Wells Mobile with Respect to Water)   | > OEWW | > FOEWW | > ROEWW  | > Based on well production and initial mobile oil saturate with respect to water. |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Recovery Efficiency (STOIIP Mobile with Respect to Gas)   | > OEIG | > FOEIG | > ROEIG  | > Based on STOIIP and initial mobile oil saturate with respect to gas.            |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Recovery Efficiency (Wells Mobile with Respect to Gas)    | > OEWG | > FOEWG | > ROEWG  | > Based on well production and initial mobile oil saturate with respect to gas.   |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| > Recovery                                                                                                                       | > Oil Production Total (Free Gas Gas)                           | > OTMF | > FOTMF | > ROTMF  | > Volumes reported at stock tank conditions.                                      |

These summary variables are computed as:

In addition to all the aforementioned summary variables, there are variables associated with specific features that may have been enabled in the input deck, for instance, the Brine Model, or the Polymer Model. The next set of sections describe the variables associated with these specific options.

\
\

### Option Specific Variables -- Alkaline Model

This feature has not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- API and Tracer Tracking

The summary variables in this section are for use for when either the API tracking model has been activated by the [API](#__RefHeading___Toc4422_421927891) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section so that the various "oil types" are tracked in the model, or for when the Tracer Model has been requested via the [TRACERS](#__RefHeading___Toc76509_327352552) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section, that defines the number of tracers in the model and the various passive tracer tracking options. Currently, only the Tracer model is implemented in OPM Flow.

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Oil API                                    | > API  | > FAPI  | > GAPI  | > [WAPI](#__RefHeading___Toc412204_2026549522) | > CAPI  | > RAPI  | > BAPI  |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Flow Rate                           | > TFR  |         |         |                                                | > CTFR  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Flow Total (Inter Region)           | > TFTT |         |         |                                                |         | > RTFTT |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Flow Total (Free Inter Region)      | > TFTF |         |         |                                                |         | > RTFTF |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Flow Total (Solution Inter Region)  | > TFTS |         |         |                                                |         | > RTFTS |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Concentration             | > TIC  | > FTIC  | > GTIC  | > WTIC                                         | > CTIC  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Concentration (Free)      | > TICF | > FTICF | > GTICF | > WTICF                                        | > CTICF |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Concentration (Solution)  | > TICS | > FTICS | > GTICS | > WTICS                                        | > CTICS |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Rate                      | > TIR  | > FTIR  | > GTIR  | > WTIR                                         | > CTIR  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Rate (Free)               | > TIRF | > FTIRF | > GTIRF | > WTIRF                                        | > CTIRF |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Rate (Solution)           | > TIRS | > FTIRS | > GTIRS | > WTIRS                                        | > CTIRS |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Total                     | > TIT  | > FTIT  | > GTIT  | > WTIT                                         | > CTIT  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Total (Free)              | > TITF | > FTITF | > GTITF | > WTITF                                        | > CTITF |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Injection Total (Solution)          | > TITS | > FTITS | > GTITS | > WTITS                                        | > CTITS |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Concentration            | > TPC  | > FTPC  | > GTPC  | > WTPC                                         | > CTPC  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Concentration (Free)     | > TPCF | > FTPCF | > GTPCF | > WTPCF                                        | > CTPCF |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Concentration (Solution) | > TPCS | > FTPCS | > GTPCS | > WTPCS                                        | > CTPCS |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Rate                     | > TPR  | > FTPR  | > GTPR  | > WTPR                                         | > CTPR  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Rate (Free)              | > TPRF | > FTPRF | > GTPRF | > WTPRF                                        | > CTPRF |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Rate (Solution)          | > TPRS | > FTPRS | > GTPRS | > WTPRS                                        | > CTPRS |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Total                    | > TPT  | > FTPT  | > GTPT  | > WTPT                                         | > CTPT  |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Total (Free)             | > TPTF | > FTPTF | > GTPTF | > WTPTF                                        | > CTPTF |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Tracer Production Total (Solution)         | > TPTS | > FTPTS | > GTPTS | > WTPTS                                        | > CTPTS |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Tracer Concentration                       | > TCN  |         |         |                                                |         |         | > BTCN  |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Tracer Concentration (Free)                | > TCNF |         |         |                                                |         |         | > BTCNF |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Tracer Concentration (Solution)            | > TCNS |         |         |                                                |         |         | > BTCNS |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Tracer In-Place                            | > TIPT | > FTIPT |         |                                                |         | > RTIPT | > BTIPT |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Tracer In-Place (Free)                     | > TIPF | > FTIPF |         |                                                |         | > RTIPF | > BTIPF |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Tracer In-Place (Solution)                 | > TIPS | > FTIPS |         |                                                |         | > RTIPS | > BTIPS |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+
| > Notes:                                                                                                                         |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
| 3)  Cells colored in gray with a mnemonic indicate that the summary variable is not available in OPM Flow.                       |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
| 4)  Cells colored in gray with no mnemonic indicate that the summary variable is not available for this combination.             |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
| 5)  Cells colored orange show combinations that are not available in OPM Flow because the underlying feature is not available.   |                                              |        |         |         |                                                |         |         |         |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+------------------------------------------------+---------+---------+---------+

::: caption
Table 11.2.11: API and Tracer Tracking Summary Variables
:::

Note that for the tracer summary variables the mnemonic should be concatenated with the tracer name as defined by the [TRACER](#__RefHeading___Toc121485_83452205) keyword in the [PROPS](#__RefHeading___Toc39329_784232322) section. This keyword defines a series of passive tracers that are associated with a phase (oil, water, or gas) in the model, see the example for reference.

#### Example

In the [PROPS](#__RefHeading___Toc39329_784232322) section the [TRACER](#__RefHeading___Toc121485_83452205) keyword defines four passive tracers one for a gas injection well, one for tracking the dissolved gas, and two to track the injected water from two water injection wells.

\-- ==============================================================================

\--

\-- PROPS SECTION

\--

\-- ==============================================================================

PROPS

\--

\-- DEFINE TRACER NAMES

\--

\-- TRACER TRACER

\-- NAME PHASE

\-- \-\-\-\-\-- \-\-\-\-\--

TRACER

\'IGS\' \'GAS\' / GAS INJECTOR

\'DGS\' \'GAS\' / DISOLVED GAS

\'IW1\' \'WAT\' / WAT INJECTOR 1

\'Iw2\' \'WAT\' / WAT INJECTOR 2

/

If we wish to report the field total amount of the tracers in-place we would use the following in the [SUMMARY](#__RefHeading___Toc43949_784232322) section:

\-- ==============================================================================

\--

\-- SUMMARY SECTION

\--

\-- ==============================================================================

SUMMARY

FTIPTIGS

FTIPTDGS

FTIPTIW1

FTIPTIW2

Note that there is no terminating "/" for field summary variables.

### Option Specific Variables -- Asphaltene Model

This feature has not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Brine Model

The available Brine model summary keywords are dependent on which form of the Brine model has been invoked in the simulation input deck. In the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section the [BRINE](#__RefHeading___Toc162083_289573908) keyword activates the standard Brine Tracking model and optionally defines the water phase to have various salinities if the [ECLMC](#__RefHeading___Toc206960_803326780) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section has been used to activate the Multi-Component Brine model. The Multi-Component Brine model allows for the water phase to have multiple water salinities.

Note that the Multi-Component Brine model is currently not supported by OPM Flow.

If OPM Flow's Salt Precipitation Model has been activated in the input deck via the [PRECSALT](#__RefHeading___Toc332782_3149455253) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section, then the Brine model summary keywords can also be employed with this option.

Note that not all these variables are available in OPM Flow; however, the simulator will issue warning messages if this is indeed the case. It is anticipated that the number of recognized summary variables will increase in future releases of OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables - CO2STORE/H2STORE Model

The variables in this section are for OPM Flow\'s black-oil [CO2STORE](#__RefHeading___Toc387968_1616145207)/[H2STORE](#REF_HEADING_KEYWORD_H2STORE) Model, and are based on the commercial simulator\'s compositional vectors (GCDI, GCDM, and WCD series), as the model is only available in the commercial simulator\'s compositional simulator.

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+-------------------+-------------------+
| > CO2STORE/H2STORE Field, Group and Well Summary Variables                                                                       |                                    |        |         |         |         |                   |                   |

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+-------------------+-------------------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Mass Injection Total  | > GMIT | > FGMIT | > GGMIT | > WGMIT | > CGMIT           | > CGMITL          |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+-------------------+-------------------+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Mass Production Rate  | > GMPR | > FGMPR | > GGMPR | > WGMPR | > CGMPR           | > CGMPRL          |

| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Mass Production Total | > GMPT | > FGMPT | > GGMPT | > WGMPT | > CGMPT           | > CGMPTL          |

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ In-place (Gas Phase)                                                          | > GMGP | > FGMGP | > RGMGP  | > BGMGP |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ In-place (Liquid Phase)                                                       | > GMDS | > FGMDS | > RGMDS  | > BGMDS |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Effectively Residual Trapped (\'Stranded\') in the gas phase                  | > GMST | > FGMST | > RGMST  | > BGMST |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Effectively Residual Untrapped (\'Unstranded\') in the gas phase              | > GMUS | > FGMUS | > RGMUS  | > BGMUS |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Maximum Potential Residual Trapped in the gas phase                           | > GMTR | > FGMTR | > RGMTR  | > BGMTR |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Maximum Potential Residual Untrapped in the gas phase                         | > GMMO | > FGMMO | > RGMMO  | > BGMMO |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Immobile in the gas phase (Non-wetting relative permeability equals zero)     | > GKTR | > FGKTR | > RGKTR  | > BGKTR |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Mass                                                                                                                           | > CO~2~/H~2~ Mobile in the gas phase (Non-wetting relative permeability greater than zero) | > GKMO | > FGKMO | > RGKMO  | > BGKMO |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Moles                                                                                                                          | > CO~2~/H~2~ Immobile in the gas phase                                                     | > GCDI | > FGCDI | > RGCDI  | > BGCDI |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Moles                                                                                                                          | > CO~2~/H~2~ Mobile in the gas phase                                                       | > GCDM | > FGCDM | > RGCDM  | > BGCDM |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Moles                                                                                                                          | > CO~2~/H~2~ Immobile in the gas phase (Non-wetting relative permeability equals zero)     | > GKDI | > FGKDI | > RGKDI  | > BGKDI |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Moles                                                                                                                          | > CO~2~/H~2~ Mobile in the gas phase (Non-wetting relative permeability greater than zero) | > GKDM | > FGKDM | > RGKDM  | > BGKDM |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Moles                                                                                                                          | > CO~2~/H~2~ Dissolved in the water phase                                                  | > WCD  | > FWCD  | > RWCD   | > BWCD  |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Water in the gas phase                                                                   | > WIPG | > FWIPG | > RWIPG  | > BWIPG |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Volume                                                                                                                         | > Water in the water phase                                                                 | > WIPL | > FWIPL | > RWIPL  | > BWIPL |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+----------+---------+
| > Notes:                                                                                                                         |                                                                                            |        |         |          |         |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                                                                            |        |         |          |         |

Table 11.2.13: CO2STORE/H2STORE Field, Region, and Block Summary Variables

See the OpenGoSim documentation (https://docs.opengosim.com/cirrus/theory/residual_and_stranded.html) for more details of how the trapped gas saturation and the stranded gas saturation contribute to the maximum potential residual trapping (GMTR) and the effective residual trapping (GMST) of CO~2~ in saline aquifers when relative permeability hysteresis is modelled.

The 11th Society of Petroleum Engineers Comparative Solution Project (http://spe.org/csp) defines the "immobile free-phase CO~2~" as "CO~2~ at saturations for which the non-wetting phase relative permeability equals zero" (GKDI, GKTR).

Note that the GK\* and GM\* series of variables are OPM Flow specific variables.

Note that the WIPG and WIPL series of variables are OPM Flow specific variables.

### Option Specific Variables -- Coal Bed Methane Model

The Coal Bed Methane model is not supported by OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Conductive Faults Model

Conductive faults have not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Environmental Tracers

Environmental tracers are not supported by OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Formation Damage Model

The variables in this section are for the OPM Flow\'s Formation Damage Model. The [WINJDAM](#REF_HEADING_KEYWORD_WINJDAM) keyword sets up the filter cake properties for the specific water injection well in the [SCHEDULE](#__RefHeading___Toc43945_784232322) section.

### Option Specific Variables -- Foam Model Tracers

The Foam phase and model are activated via the [FOAM](#__RefHeading___Toc171586_289573908) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section. Note in the commercial simulator the [FOAM](#__RefHeading___Toc171586_289573908) phase and model can be used in conjunction with the [POLYMER](#__RefHeading___Toc38609_2267116897) and [SURFACT](#__RefHeading___Toc863854_4250154414) phases; this is not the case for OPM Flow. OPM Flow's [FOAM](#__RefHeading___Toc171586_289573908) phase and model is a standalone implementation and cannot be used in conjunction with the either the [POLYMER](#__RefHeading___Toc38609_2267116897) or [SURFACT](#__RefHeading___Toc863854_4250154414) phases.

::: caption
Table 11.2.15: Foam Model Tracers Summary Variables
:::

Note that not all these variables are available in OPM Flow; however, the simulator will issue warning messages if this is indeed the case. It is anticipated that the number of recognized summary variables will increase in future releases of OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Gas Field Operations Model

The Gas Field Operations model has not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Gas Lift Optimization Model

For the Gas Lift Optimization model only a few [SUMMARY](#__RefHeading___Toc43949_784232322) vectors are available, both in OPM Flow and the commercial simulator, as depicted in . Gas lift optimization is activated by the [LIFTOPT](#__RefHeading___Toc118992_332691817) keyword in the [SCHEDULE](#__RefHeading___Toc43945_784232322) section as gas lift activation can vary through time depending on the flow characteristics of the wells.

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+----+----+----+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Gas lift gas rate, based on ALQ                                                                                              | > GLIR | > FGLIR | > GGLIR | > WGLIR |    |    |    |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+----+----+----+
| > Flow                                                                                                                           | > Incremental oil rate per unit of incremental gas lift gas quantity, that is the well's gradient as defined by equation below | > OGLR |         |         | > WOGLR |    |    |    |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+----+----+----+
| > Notes:                                                                                                                         |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
| 3)  Cells colored in gray with a mnemonic indicate that the summary variable is not available in OPM Flow.                       |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
| 4)  Cells colored in gray with no mnemonic indicate that the summary variable is not available for this combination.             |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
|                                                                                                                                  |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
| 5)  Cells colored orange show combinations that are not available in OPM Flow because the underlying feature is not available.   |                                                                                                                                |        |         |         |         |    |    |    |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------+---------+---------+---------+----+----+----+

Table 11.2.16: Gas Lift Optimization Model Summary Variables

The incremental gas lift gas supply is allocated to a well based on the well's current incremental gradient using the following formulae:

where

β~w~ = a weighting factor for the preferential allocation of lift gas,

β~g~ = the gas production rate weighting factor,

∆Q~Oil~ = the increment/decrement in oil production rate,

∆Q~Gas~ = the increment/decrement in gas production rate, and

∆Q~GasLift~ = the increment/decrement in gas lift gas rate.

Normally β~g~ is defaulted to zero and in which case equation reduces to:

Note that if gas lift optimization has been activated in the model then the gas production [SUMMARY](#__RefHeading___Toc43949_784232322) variables (FGPR, GGPR, WGPR, FGPT, etc.) only contain the produced gas volumes, that is the reported values exclude the gas associated with gas lift gas.

Secondly, the well gas lift rates are adjusted by the well efficiencies in the calculating the group and field gas lift rates.

### Option Specific Variables -- Gas Calorific Value Reporting

This feature has not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Gi Psuedo-Compositional Model

This feature has not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- LGR and Coarsening

Local Grid Refinement ("LGR") and cell coarsening have not been implemented in OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- Biofilm And MICP Model

The [MICP](#__RefHeading___Toc383375_111689907) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section activates the Microbially Induced Calcite Precipitation ("MICP") model for the run. The summary variables for this option are outlined in . Summary variables related to microbial and biofilm quantities can be also used with the [BIOFILM](#REF_HEADING_KEYWORD_BIOFILM) model.

### Option Specific Variables -- Multi-Segment Wells

The summary variables in this section are for use for when multi-segment wells are active in the model, and the variables only apply to the well segments requested for a multi-segment well, not to the well, well connection, or well completion.

Note that not all these variables are available in OPM Flow; however, the simulator will issue warning messages if this is indeed the case. It is anticipated that the number of recognized summary variables will increase in future releases of OPM Flow.

::: caption
Table 11.2.17: Multi-Segment Wells Summary Variables
:::

#### Examples

For example, to get the segment oil flow rates for well OP01 segments two, three, and four and for segment two for OP02 one would use:

\-- ==============================================================================

\--

\-- SUMMARY SECTION

\--

\-- ==============================================================================

SUMMARY

SOFR

'OP01' 2 /

'OP01' 3 /

'OP01' 4 /

'OP02' 2 /

/

or to get all the oil flow rates for all the segments for well OP01:

\-- ==============================================================================

\--

\-- SUMMARY SECTION

\--

\-- ==============================================================================

SUMMARY

SOFR

'OP01' /

/

Care should be exercised when defaulting the list of wells and segments as there is the potential to generate large volumes of data.

### Option Specific Variables -- Network Model

For the Network models only a few [SUMMARY](#__RefHeading___Toc43949_784232322) vectors for groups and nodes are available, both in OPM Flow and the commercial simulator, as depicted in . There are two types of network option in the simulator: a Standard Network and an Extended Network option, the latter is activated by the [NETWORK](#__RefHeading___Toc311583_1841740821) keyword in the [RUNSPEC](#__RefHeading___Toc55591_1778172979) section. The summary vectors apply to both the Standard and Extended Network options.

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----+----+----------+----+----+----+----+
| > Pressure                                                                                                                       | > Group/Node pressure in a production network based on rates at end of timestep (OPM Flow specific). An alias for NPR. |    |    | > GNETPR |    |    |    |    |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----+----+----------+----+----+----+----+
| > Pressure                                                                                                                       | > Group/Node pressure in a production network.                                                                         |    |    | > GPR    |    |    |    |    |

| > Pressure                                                                                                                       | > Group/Node pressure in a water injection network.                                                                    |    |    | > GPRW   |    |    |    |    |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----+----+----------+----+----+----+----+
| > Pressure                                                                                                                       | > Pressure drop along the group's or node's outlet branch in a production network.                                     |    |    | > GPRB   |    |    |    |    |

| > Pressure                                                                                                                       | > Pressure drop along the group's or node's inlet branch in a water injection network.                                 |    |    | > GPRBW  |    |    |    |    |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----+----+----------+----+----+----+----+
| > Pressure                                                                                                                       | > Group/Node pressure in a production network based on rates at end of timestep (OPM Flow specific).                   |    |    | > NPR    |    |    |    |    |

Table 11.2.18: Network Model Summary Variables

Note that not all these variables are available in OPM Flow; however, the simulator will issue warning messages if this is indeed the case. It is anticipated that the number of recognized summary variables will increase in future releases of OPM Flow.

### Option Specific Variables -- OPM Flow Simulation Performance

The following table () lists the OPM Flow simulation performance summary variables that can be written to the SUMMARY file. Note that not all these variables are available in OPM Flow; however, the simulator will issue warning messages if this is indeed the case. It is anticipated that the number of recognized summary variables will increase in future releases of OPM Flow.

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

| > Iterations - Total number of linear iterations for each gradient pressure (Gradient Option).                                                                                                                                  | > HSUMLINS                                      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |

| > Maximum Courant-Friedrichs-Lewy value for each time step.                                                                                                                                                                     | > MAXCFL                                        | > Compositional keyword.                                                                                                                                                                                                        |

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
